# Jogg API Video Generation Options

## Basic Parameters

### Aspect Ratio
- 0: [9:16] (Portrait/Mobile)
- 1: [16:9] (Landscape)
- 2: [1:1] (Square)

### Video Length
- 15 seconds
- 30 seconds
- 60 seconds

### Language
Default: english
